## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Trace usage/callers | `sg_find_references` |
| See implementation | `sg_go_to_definition` |
| Read full file | `sg_read_file` |
| Browse structure | `sg_list_files` |
| Find repos | `sg_list_repos` |
| Search commits | `sg_commit_search` |
| Track changes | `sg_diff_search` |
| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

# gRPC Health Checking and Keepalive Protocol Implementation

## Your Task

Find all C++ source and header files in grpc/grpc that implement the health checking service and keepalive mechanism. Identify: the health checking service implementation under src/cpp/server/health/, the keepalive timer logic in src/core/ext/transport/chttp2/, the client-side health checking channel filter, the server-side keepalive enforcement policy, and the connectivity watcher. For each file report the path and primary class or function.

## Context

You are working on a codebase task involving repos from the org domain.

## Available Resources

The local `/workspace/` directory contains: sg-evals/grpc--v1.68.0.

492026-03-08T19:30:56.749743agentmessage-
The answer.json file has been created successfully. Here's a summary of my findings:

## Summary of Findings

### Health Checking Service (`src/cpp/server/health/`)
- **`default_health_check_service.h/.cc`** — Primary class: `DefaultHealthCheckService` with nested `HealthCheckServiceImpl` (handles Check/Watch RPCs) and `WatchReactor` (manages streaming Watch responses)
- **`health_check_service.cc`** — `EnableDefaultHealthCheckService()` global toggle
- **`health_check_service_server_builder_option.cc`** — `HealthCheckServiceServerBuilderOption` for registering custom health check services

### Keepalive Timer Logic (`src/core/ext/transport/chttp2/`)
- **`internal.h`** — `grpc_chttp2_transport` struct with keepalive fields; `grpc_chttp2_keepalive_state` enum (WAITING/PINGING/DYING/DISABLED)
- **`chttp2_transport.cc`** — Core keepalive functions: `init_keepalive_ping_locked()`, `finish_keepalive_ping_locked()`, `maybe_reset_keepalive_ping_timer_locked()`
- **`writing.cc`** — Sets up keepalive ping timeout timer
- **`ping_abuse_policy.h/.cc`** — `Chttp2PingAbusePolicy` (server-side keepalive enforcement, tracks ping strikes)
- **`ping_rate_policy.h/.cc`** — `Chttp2PingRatePolicy` (client-side ping rate limiting)
- **`ping_callbacks.h/.cc`** — `Chttp2PingCallbacks` (manages in-flight ping lifecycle)

(after handshake).\\n44: * What happens when the keepalive timer fires?\\n45:   * When the keepalive timer fires, gRPC Core will try to send a keepalive ping on the transport. It is sent periodically, and if the ping is not acknowledged by the peer within a certain timeout period, the transport is disconnected.\\n4: \\n5: This guide documents the knobs within gRPC core to control the current behavior of the keepalive ping.\\n6: \\n7: The keepalive ping in core is controlled by the following channel arguments -\\n8: \\n9: * **GRPC_ARG_KEEPALIVE_TIME_MS**\\n10:   * This channel argument controls the period (in milliseconds) after which a keepalive ping is sent on the transport.\\n11: * **GRPC_ARG_KEEPALIVE_TIMEOUT_MS**\\n12:   * This channel argument controls the amount of time (in milliseconds) the sender of the keepalive ping waits for an acknowledgement.
